<UserId.>116565547507981160575</UserId.>< review>
Tiny and VERY compelling.  I don't really know how to deconvolve the particular exhibits that were there from the museum at large, as it's my first time, but their choices of exhibits were absolutely phenomenal. The pictures simply don't do them justice, but they all had a presence of their own, saying and whispering and singing and showing you lifetimes of stories.<//review>

< Rating>
5</Rating>
< Text>
Whenever I am in CA I made a trip down to San Jose specifically to see the quilt museum. I don't quilt, but I do collect fabric art and own quilts from the 1880s to now. Each show is worthwhile. I admire the creativity of the various artists and what they make. Not all are quilts. They normally display some of the historic quilts along with the contemporary fabric art. It's a small museum, so go down the block to the other galleries. Then see the San Jose Art museum and enjoy the restaurants in the area too. Christmas in downtown SJ is an annual event.<//Text>

<rating>5</rating>< Review>
(Translated by Google) Amazing, colorful and unusual. Best regards to people keeping and restoring traditional crafts!
An amazing place full of bright colors, where traditions are preserved and new generations are taught such crafts as quilting (in Russian patch-work) and weaving. It was interesting to encounter the little-known tradition of weaving the numerous May tribes. I highly recommend visiting and gaining vivid impressions.

(Original)
Amazing, colorful and unusual. Best regards to people keeping and restoring traditional crafts!
Удивительное, полное ярких красок место, где сохраняют традиции и обучают новые поколения таким ремеслам, как quilting (на русском патч-ворк) и ткачество. Интересно было столкнуться с мало известной мне традицией ткачества многочисленных племён Мая. Очень рекомендую побывать и набраться ярких впечатлений.</Review>

< review>
Can always trust the quality and service to be great at any Intelligentsia.

Bought their Summer Solstice blend which the barista told me is fruity, great for some cold brew at home in this 90 degree weather.

Also got their Limelight that they sell during the summertime. Very delicious and refreshing for being an iced coffee drink.

Interior is clean and professional. Can do some serious work here if needed, but also edgy enough to have a casual conversation.

They care for the environment by raising awareness from the usage of straws.

Their espresso drinks are solid and sophisticated.

Have not tried their teas, only coffee.< /review>

< review>
This review isn't on their store but is on their online website and service on making a purchase.  In addition, I'm also reviewing the products as well......

After purchasing a new truck, I was looking for a good sealant and polish to shine it up.  After doing a lot research, I chose Adam's products and very glad I did.  I purchased the Polish, Clay Bars, and Graphene Spray (Not the concentrate).  The truck has never looked better and it keeps a glare on it even after a solid rain.  The polish and clay bar are self explanatory but the Graphene spray was definitely the prize of the lot.

Application was easy (and I'm not a pro detailer) and I went with the spray in case I made mistakes.  I've even had neighbors stop by to ask what I used on the truck.  After a wash, I do coat it down with the "graphene" detail spray and the shine pops back just like it was freshly polished.  I couldn't be happier with the purchase.

Online purchase was easy and shipping was within 24 hours.  Because they have to use UPS for liquids, shipping time can be a few days but that's no fault of Adam's......

Keep it up and you have a new follower!<//review>
